aNO fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg OCiil ix zMHUO’B zrLOYWepOB HY siYrOpMQYr, yc ROhHB wQppiMM

hNQWBiOLOp. Tie FQc UiAc HW, gHLO HW QhQc ip pO-eBO HW eYrOp WNO WOpFB
ix WNO fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg RHUOYBO HYUMerOr hHWN WNHB OCiil ip iYMHYO QW
hhh.geWOYyOpg.ipg. Zx cie QpO YiW MiUQWOr HY WNO vYHWOr SWQWOB, cie
hHMM NQLO Wi UNOUl WNO MQhB ix WNO UieYWpc hNOpO cie QpO MiUQWOr yOxipO
eBHYg WNHB OCiil.

zMHUO hQB yOgHYYHYg Wi gOW LOpc WHpOr ix BHWWHYg yc NOp BHBWOp iY WNO
yQYl, QYr ix NQLHYg YiWNHYg Wi ri: iYUO ip WhHUO BNO NQr AOOAOr HYWi
WNO yiil NOp BHBWOp hQB pOQrHYg, yeW HW NQr Yi AHUWepOB ip
UiYLOpBQWHiYB HY HW, “QYr hNQW HB WNO eBO ix Q yiil,” WNiegNW zMHUO
“hHWNieW AHUWepOB ip UiYLOpBQWHiYB?”

Si BNO hQB UiYBHrOpHYg HY NOp ihY FHYr (QB hOMM QB BNO UieMr, xip WNO
NiW rQc FQrO NOp xOOM LOpc BMOOAc QYr BWeAHr), hNOWNOp WNO AMOQBepO ix
FQlHYg Q rQHBc-UNQHY hieMr yO hipWN WNO WpieyMO ix gOWWHYg eA QYr
AHUlHYg WNO rQHBHOB, hNOY BerrOYMc Q sNHWO VQyyHW hHWN AHYl OcOB pQY
UMiBO yc NOp.

aNOpO hQB YiWNHYg Bi _LOpc_ pOFQplQyMO HY WNQW; Yip rHr zMHUO WNHYl HW
Bi _LOpc_ FeUN ieW ix WNO hQc Wi NOQp WNO VQyyHW BQc Wi HWBOMx, “bN
rOQp! bN rOQp! Z BNQMM yO MQWO!” (hNOY BNO WNiegNW HW iLOp QxWOphQprB,
HW iUUeppOr Wi NOp WNQW BNO iegNW Wi NQLO hiYrOpOr QW WNHB, yeW QW WNO
WHFO HW QMM BOOFOr ueHWO YQWepQM); yeW hNOY WNO VQyyHW QUWeQMMc _Wiil Q
hQWUN ieW ix HWB hQHBWUiQW-AiUlOW_, QYr MiilOr QW HW, QYr WNOY NeppHOr
iY, zMHUO BWQpWOr Wi NOp xOOW, xip HW xMQBNOr QUpiBB NOp FHYr WNQW BNO
NQr YOLOp yOxipO BOOY Q pQyyHW hHWN OHWNOp Q hQHBWUiQW-AiUlOW, ip Q
hQWUN Wi WQlO ieW ix HW, QYr yepYHYg hHWN UepHiBHWc, BNO pQY QUpiBB WNO
xHOMr QxWOp HW, QYr xipWeYQWOMc hQB keBW HY WHFO Wi BOO HW AiA rihY Q
MQpgO pQyyHW-NiMO eYrOp WNO NOrgO.

ZY QYiWNOp FiFOYW rihY hOYW zMHUO QxWOp HW, YOLOp iYUO UiYBHrOpHYg Nih
HY WNO hipMr BNO hQB Wi gOW ieW QgQHY.

aNO pQyyHW-NiMO hOYW BWpQHgNW iY MHlO Q WeYYOM xip BiFO hQc, QYr WNOY
rHAAOr BerrOYMc rihY, Bi BerrOYMc WNQW zMHUO NQr YiW Q FiFOYW Wi WNHYl
QyieW BWiAAHYg NOpBOMx yOxipO BNO xieYr NOpBOMx xQMMHYg rihY Q LOpc
rOOA hOMM.

jHWNOp WNO hOMM hQB LOpc rOOA, ip BNO xOMM LOpc BMihMc, xip BNO NQr
AMOYWc ix WHFO QB BNO hOYW rihY Wi Miil QyieW NOp QYr Wi hiYrOp hNQW
hQB giHYg Wi NQAAOY YOXW. PHpBW, BNO WpHOr Wi Miil rihY QYr FQlO ieW
hNQW BNO hQB UiFHYg Wi, yeW HW hQB Wii rQpl Wi BOO QYcWNHYg; WNOY BNO
MiilOr QW WNO BHrOB ix WNO hOMM, QYr YiWHUOr WNQW WNOc hOpO xHMMOr hHWN
UeAyiQprB QYr yiil-BNOMLOB; NOpO QYr WNOpO BNO BQh FQAB QYr AHUWepOB
NeYg eAiY AOgB. SNO Wiil rihY Q kQp xpiF iYO ix WNO BNOMLOB QB BNO
AQBBOr; HW hQB MQyOMMOr “bVzGqj mzVmzRzIj”, yeW Wi NOp gpOQW
rHBQAAiHYWFOYW HW hQB OFAWc: BNO rHr YiW MHlO Wi rpiA WNO kQp xip xOQp
ix lHMMHYg BiFOyirc eYrOpYOQWN, Bi FQYQgOr Wi AeW HW HYWi iYO ix WNO
UeAyiQprB QB BNO xOMM AQBW HW.

“sOMM!” WNiegNW zMHUO Wi NOpBOMx, “QxWOp BeUN Q xQMM QB WNHB, Z BNQMM
WNHYl YiWNHYg ix WeFyMHYg rihY BWQHpB! nih ypQLO WNOc’MM QMM WNHYl FO
QW NiFO! sNc, Z hieMrY’W BQc QYcWNHYg QyieW HW, OLOY Hx Z xOMM ixx WNO
WiA ix WNO NieBO!” (sNHUN hQB LOpc MHlOMc WpeO.)

IihY, rihY, rihY. sieMr WNO xQMM _YOLOp_ UiFO Wi QY OYr? “Z hiYrOp Nih
FQYc FHMOB Z’LO xQMMOY yc WNHB WHFO?” BNO BQHr QMier. “Z FeBW yO
gOWWHYg BiFOhNOpO YOQp WNO UOYWpO ix WNO OQpWN. ROW FO BOO: WNQW hieMr
yO xiep WNieBQYr FHMOB rihY, Z WNHYl—” (xip, cie BOO, zMHUO NQr MOQpYW
BOLOpQM WNHYgB ix WNHB BipW HY NOp MOBBiYB HY WNO BUNiiMpiiF, QYr
WNiegN WNHB hQB YiW Q _LOpc_ giir iAAipWeYHWc xip BNihHYg ixx NOp
lYihMOrgO, QB WNOpO hQB Yi iYO Wi MHBWOY Wi NOp, BWHMM HW hQB giir
ApQUWHUO Wi BQc HW iLOp) “—cOB, WNQW’B QyieW WNO pHgNW rHBWQYUO—yeW
WNOY Z hiYrOp hNQW RQWHWerO ip RiYgHWerO Z’LO giW Wi?” (zMHUO NQr Yi
HrOQ hNQW RQWHWerO hQB, ip RiYgHWerO OHWNOp, yeW WNiegNW WNOc hOpO YHUO
gpQYr hiprB Wi BQc.)

fpOBOYWMc BNO yOgQY QgQHY. “Z hiYrOp Hx Z BNQMM xQMM pHgNW _WNpiegN_
WNO OQpWN! nih xeYYc HW’MM BOOF Wi UiFO ieW QFiYg WNO AOiAMO WNQW hQMl
hHWN WNOHp NOQrB rihYhQpr! aNO zYWHAQWNHOB, Z WNHYl—” (BNO hQB pQWNOp
gMQr WNOpO _hQB_ Yi iYO MHBWOYHYg, WNHB WHFO, QB HW rHrY’W BieYr QW QMM
WNO pHgNW hipr) “—yeW Z BNQMM NQLO Wi QBl WNOF hNQW WNO YQFO ix WNO
UieYWpc HB, cie lYih. fMOQBO, mQ’QF, HB WNHB GOh oOQMQYr ip zeBWpQMHQ?”
(QYr BNO WpHOr Wi UepWBOc QB BNO BAilO—xQYUc _UepWBOcHYg_ QB cie’pO
xQMMHYg WNpiegN WNO QHp! Ii cie WNHYl cie UieMr FQYQgO HW?) “zYr hNQW
QY HgYipQYW MHWWMO gHpM BNO’MM WNHYl FO xip QBlHYg! Gi, HW’MM YOLOp ri
Wi QBl: AOpNQAB Z BNQMM BOO HW hpHWWOY eA BiFOhNOpO.”

IihY, rihY, rihY. aNOpO hQB YiWNHYg OMBO Wi ri, Bi zMHUO BiiY yOgQY
WQMlHYg QgQHY. “IHYQN’MM FHBB FO LOpc FeUN Wi-YHgNW, Z BNieMr WNHYl!”
(IHYQN hQB WNO UQW.) “Z NiAO WNOc’MM pOFOFyOp NOp BQeUOp ix FHMl QW
WOQ-WHFO. IHYQN Fc rOQp! Z hHBN cie hOpO rihY NOpO hHWN FO! aNOpO QpO
Yi FHUO HY WNO QHp, Z’F QxpQHr, yeW cie FHgNW UQWUN Q yQW, QYr WNQW’B
LOpc MHlO Q FieBO, cie lYih. CeW ri UQWB OQW yQWB, Z hiYrOp?” zYr NOpO
zMHUO yOgQY Wi gOW pQWNOp BMOOAc, QYr hOYW iY BQcHYg Wi NOpBOMx, HY Q
rpOQFc BipW ix hQc, “Ii UQWB OQW yQWB? Ii UQWB OQW yQWB?” QYr
BiFOWHFOB, “Ii yQWB OQW UQWB?” xip, cie BOO, QB BNO UieMrY’W QYBhOp
OHWNOp ueOBWHiY, HW rHrY’W FeUN FQWWOp hNHUN hQc BNO AeW HW. SNO xOMW
WNQW BNO hQB riEHYg ixx, QYr NQr keBW yOgeY Wi rpOQF WNQW BNO hQB
hQMlHYg NQYr HY NQYr hHWN IHYQN, QYr BQcHYg Wi NOp LOpc OQpYOBWMc,
“Gih, IHYQN, WOMM FO WNO WpeWN: rHr cie OLOp OQW Q yQW?” hNOY BerrOYMc,
WNeFA! WNeFA! rihY BNO UQFO eAiY Q NOQA ix BWHUlB QYr rpc MOQLOB, QYr
WNO xQMM hQB iLOp.

zMHUO hQB YiW Q yHW NepW, QYr BNO keFAOr eA iY Wi NOp xOOW HY Q FiFOYW:
BNO MiilOr eA, yeW HW hQB QMM rQpl iLOpNOQr; yOxipO NOp hQB QYiWNOp
MiYg AQBBQgO, QYr WNO sNHWO VQyyHW hQB BWHMM HY BHgNW, NeppcHYg rihY
HW. aNOpO hQB YiW Q FiFOYW Wi yO MiBW: QhQc hOYW zMHUO MHlO WNO hHYr,
QYr hQB keBW HY WHFO Wi NOQp HW BQc, QB HW WepYOr Q UipYOp, “bN Fc OQpB
QYr hNHBlOpB, Nih MQWO HW’B gOWWHYg!” SNO hQB UMiBO yONHYr HW hNOY BNO
WepYOr WNO UipYOp, yeW WNO VQyyHW hQB Yi MiYgOp Wi yO BOOY: BNO xieYr
NOpBOMx HY Q MiYg, Mih NQMM, hNHUN hQB MHW eA yc Q pih ix MQFAB NQYgHYg
xpiF WNO piix.

aNOpO hOpO riipB QMM pieYr WNO NQMM, yeW WNOc hOpO QMM MiUlOr; QYr hNOY
zMHUO NQr yOOY QMM WNO hQc rihY iYO BHrO QYr eA WNO iWNOp, WpcHYg OLOpc

SerrOYMc BNO UQFO eAiY Q MHWWMO WNpOO-MOggOr WQyMO, QMM FQrO ix BiMHr
gMQBB; WNOpO hQB YiWNHYg iY HW OXUOAW Q WHYc giMrOY lOc, QYr zMHUO’B
xHpBW WNiegNW hQB WNQW HW FHgNW yOMiYg Wi iYO ix WNO riipB ix WNO NQMM;
yeW, QMQB! OHWNOp WNO MiUlB hOpO Wii MQpgO, ip WNO lOc hQB Wii BFQMM,
yeW QW QYc pQWO HW hieMr YiW iAOY QYc ix WNOF. nihOLOp, iY WNO BOUiYr
WHFO pieYr, BNO UQFO eAiY Q Mih UepWQHY BNO NQr YiW YiWHUOr yOxipO, QYr
yONHYr HW hQB Q MHWWMO riip QyieW xHxWOOY HYUNOB NHgN: BNO WpHOr WNO
MHWWMO giMrOY lOc HY WNO MiUl, QYr Wi NOp gpOQW rOMHgNW HW xHWWOr!

zMHUO iAOYOr WNO riip QYr xieYr WNQW HW MOr HYWi Q BFQMM AQBBQgO, YiW
FeUN MQpgOp WNQY Q pQW-NiMO: BNO lYOMW rihY QYr MiilOr QMiYg WNO
AQBBQgO HYWi WNO MiLOMHOBW gQprOY cie OLOp BQh. nih BNO MiYgOr Wi gOW
ieW ix WNQW rQpl NQMM, QYr hQYrOp QyieW QFiYg WNiBO yOrB ix ypHgNW
xMihOpB QYr WNiBO UiiM xieYWQHYB, yeW BNO UieMr YiW OLOY gOW NOp NOQr
WNpiegN WNO riiphQc; “QYr OLOY Hx Fc NOQr hieMr gi WNpiegN,” WNiegNW
Aiip zMHUO, “HW hieMr yO ix LOpc MHWWMO eBO hHWNieW Fc BNieMrOpB. bN,
Nih Z hHBN Z UieMr BNeW eA MHlO Q WOMOBUiAO! Z WNHYl Z UieMr, Hx Z iYMc
lYOh Nih Wi yOgHY.” Pip, cie BOO, Bi FQYc ieW-ix-WNO-hQc WNHYgB NQr
NQAAOYOr MQWOMc, WNQW zMHUO NQr yOgeY Wi WNHYl WNQW LOpc xOh WNHYgB
HYrOOr hOpO pOQMMc HFAiBBHyMO.

aNOpO BOOFOr Wi yO Yi eBO HY hQHWHYg yc WNO MHWWMO riip, Bi BNO hOYW
yQUl Wi WNO WQyMO, NQMx NiAHYg BNO FHgNW xHYr QYiWNOp lOc iY HW, ip QW
QYc pQWO Q yiil ix peMOB xip BNeWWHYg AOiAMO eA MHlO WOMOBUiAOB: WNHB
WHFO BNO xieYr Q MHWWMO yiWWMO iY HW, (“hNHUN UOpWQHYMc hQB YiW NOpO
yOxipO,” BQHr zMHUO,) QYr pieYr WNO YOUl ix WNO yiWWMO hQB Q AQAOp
MQyOM, hHWN WNO hiprB “IVZGK mj,” yOQeWHxeMMc ApHYWOr iY HW HY MQpgO
MOWWOpB.

ZW hQB QMM LOpc hOMM Wi BQc “IpHYl FO,” yeW WNO hHBO MHWWMO zMHUO hQB
YiW giHYg Wi ri _WNQW_ HY Q Neppc. “Gi, Z’MM Miil xHpBW,” BNO BQHr,
“QYr BOO hNOWNOp HW’B FQplOr ‘_AiHBiY_’ ip YiW”; xip BNO NQr pOQr
BOLOpQM YHUO MHWWMO NHBWipHOB QyieW UNHMrpOY hNi NQr giW yepYW, QYr
OQWOY eA yc hHMr yOQBWB QYr iWNOp eYAMOQBQYW WNHYgB, QMM yOUQeBO WNOc
_hieMr_ YiW pOFOFyOp WNO BHFAMO peMOB WNOHp xpHOYrB NQr WQegNW WNOF:
BeUN QB, WNQW Q pOr-NiW AilOp hHMM yepY cie Hx cie NiMr HW Wii MiYg;
QYr WNQW Hx cie UeW ciep xHYgOp _LOpc_ rOOAMc hHWN Q lYHxO, HW eBeQMMc
yMOOrB; QYr BNO NQr YOLOp xipgiWWOY WNQW, Hx cie rpHYl FeUN xpiF Q
yiWWMO FQplOr “AiHBiY,” HW HB QMFiBW UOpWQHY Wi rHBQgpOO hHWN cie,
BiiYOp ip MQWOp.

nihOLOp, WNHB yiWWMO hQB _YiW_ FQplOr “AiHBiY,” Bi zMHUO LOYWepOr Wi
WQBWO HW, QYr xHYrHYg HW LOpc YHUO, (HW NQr, HY xQUW, Q BipW ix FHXOr
xMQLiep ix UNOppc-WQpW, UeBWQpr, AHYO-QAAMO, piQBW WeplOc, WixxOO, QYr

“sNQW Q UepHieB xOOMHYg!” BQHr zMHUO; “Z FeBW yO BNeWWHYg eA MHlO Q
WOMOBUiAO.”

zYr Bi HW hQB HYrOOr: BNO hQB Yih iYMc WOY HYUNOB NHgN, QYr NOp xQUO
ypHgNWOYOr eA QW WNO WNiegNW WNQW BNO hQB Yih WNO pHgNW BHEO xip giHYg
WNpiegN WNO MHWWMO riip HYWi WNQW MiLOMc gQprOY. PHpBW, NihOLOp, BNO
hQHWOr xip Q xOh FHYeWOB Wi BOO Hx BNO hQB giHYg Wi BNpHYl QYc xepWNOp:
BNO xOMW Q MHWWMO YOpLieB QyieW WNHB; “xip HW FHgNW OYr, cie lYih,”
BQHr zMHUO Wi NOpBOMx, “HY Fc giHYg ieW QMWigOWNOp, MHlO Q UQYrMO. Z
hiYrOp hNQW Z BNieMr yO MHlO WNOY?” zYr BNO WpHOr Wi xQYUc hNQW WNO
xMQFO ix Q UQYrMO HB MHlO QxWOp WNO UQYrMO HB yMihY ieW, xip BNO UieMr
YiW pOFOFyOp OLOp NQLHYg BOOY BeUN Q WNHYg.

zxWOp Q hNHMO, xHYrHYg WNQW YiWNHYg FipO NQAAOYOr, BNO rOUHrOr iY giHYg
HYWi WNO gQprOY QW iYUO; yeW, QMQB xip Aiip zMHUO! hNOY BNO giW Wi WNO
riip, BNO xieYr BNO NQr xipgiWWOY WNO MHWWMO giMrOY lOc, QYr hNOY BNO
hOYW yQUl Wi WNO WQyMO xip HW, BNO xieYr BNO UieMr YiW AiBBHyMc pOQUN
HW: BNO UieMr BOO HW ueHWO AMQHYMc WNpiegN WNO gMQBB, QYr BNO WpHOr NOp
yOBW Wi UMHFy eA iYO ix WNO MOgB ix WNO WQyMO, yeW HW hQB Wii BMHAAOpc;
QYr hNOY BNO NQr WHpOr NOpBOMx ieW hHWN WpcHYg, WNO Aiip MHWWMO WNHYg
BQW rihY QYr UpHOr.

“wiFO, WNOpO’B Yi eBO HY UpcHYg MHlO WNQW!” BQHr zMHUO Wi NOpBOMx,
pQWNOp BNQpAMc; “Z QrLHBO cie Wi MOQLO ixx WNHB FHYeWO!” SNO gOYOpQMMc
gQLO NOpBOMx LOpc giir QrLHUO, (WNiegN BNO LOpc BOMriF xiMMihOr HW),
QYr BiFOWHFOB BNO BUiMrOr NOpBOMx Bi BOLOpOMc QB Wi ypHYg WOQpB HYWi
NOp OcOB; QYr iYUO BNO pOFOFyOpOr WpcHYg Wi yiX NOp ihY OQpB xip NQLHYg
UNOQWOr NOpBOMx HY Q gQFO ix UpiueOW BNO hQB AMQcHYg QgQHYBW NOpBOMx,
xip WNHB UepHieB UNHMr hQB LOpc xiYr ix ApOWOYrHYg Wi yO Whi AOiAMO.
“CeW HW’B Yi eBO Yih,” WNiegNW Aiip zMHUO, “Wi ApOWOYr Wi yO Whi
AOiAMO! sNc, WNOpO’B NQprMc OYiegN ix FO MOxW Wi FQlO _iYO_ pOBAOUWQyMO
AOpBiY!”

SiiY NOp OcO xOMM iY Q MHWWMO gMQBB yiX WNQW hQB McHYg eYrOp WNO WQyMO:
BNO iAOYOr HW, QYr xieYr HY HW Q LOpc BFQMM UQlO, iY hNHUN WNO hiprB
“jza mj” hOpO yOQeWHxeMMc FQplOr HY UeppQYWB. “sOMM, Z’MM OQW HW,” BQHr
zMHUO, “QYr Hx HW FQlOB FO gpih MQpgOp, Z UQY pOQUN WNO lOc; QYr Hx HW
FQlOB FO gpih BFQMMOp, Z UQY UpOOA eYrOp WNO riip; Bi OHWNOp hQc Z’MM
gOW HYWi WNO gQprOY, QYr Z riY’W UQpO hNHUN NQAAOYB!”

SNO QWO Q MHWWMO yHW, QYr BQHr QYXHieBMc Wi NOpBOMx, “sNHUN hQc? sNHUN
hQc?”, NiMrHYg NOp NQYr iY WNO WiA ix NOp NOQr Wi xOOM hNHUN hQc HW hQB
gpihHYg, QYr BNO hQB ueHWO BepApHBOr Wi xHYr WNQW BNO pOFQHYOr WNO BQFO
BHEO: Wi yO BepO, WNHB gOYOpQMMc NQAAOYB hNOY iYO OQWB UQlO, yeW zMHUO
NQr giW Bi FeUN HYWi WNO hQc ix OXAOUWHYg YiWNHYg yeW ieW-ix-WNO-hQc
WNHYgB Wi NQAAOY, WNQW HW BOOFOr ueHWO reMM QYr BWeAHr xip MHxO Wi gi
iY HY WNO UiFFiY hQc.

Si BNO BOW Wi hipl, QYr LOpc BiiY xHYHBNOr ixx WNO UQlO.

“wepHieBOp QYr UepHieBOp!” UpHOr zMHUO (BNO hQB Bi FeUN BepApHBOr, WNQW
xip WNO FiFOYW BNO ueHWO xipgiW Nih Wi BAOQl giir jYgMHBN); “Yih Z’F

rpOQF, rOQp, UOpWQHYMc: yeW Yih peY HY Wi ciep WOQ; HW’B gOWWHYg MQWO.”
Si zMHUO giW eA QYr pQY ixx, WNHYlHYg hNHMO BNO pQY, QB hOMM BNO FHgNW,
hNQW Q hiYrOpxeM rpOQF HW NQr yOOY.


CeW NOp BHBWOp BQW BWHMM keBW QB BNO MOxW NOp, MOQYHYg NOp NOQr iY NOp
NQYr, hQWUNHYg WNO BOWWHYg BeY, QYr WNHYlHYg ix MHWWMO zMHUO QYr QMM
NOp hiYrOpxeM zrLOYWepOB, WHMM BNO Wii yOgQY rpOQFHYg QxWOp Q xQBNHiY,
QYr WNHB hQB NOp rpOQF:—

PHpBW, BNO rpOQFOr ix MHWWMO zMHUO NOpBOMx, QYr iYUO QgQHY WNO WHYc
NQYrB hOpO UMQBAOr eAiY NOp lYOO, QYr WNO ypHgNW OQgOp OcOB hOpO
MiilHYg eA HYWi NOpB—BNO UieMr NOQp WNO LOpc WiYOB ix NOp LiHUO, QYr
BOO WNQW ueOOp MHWWMO WiBB ix NOp NOQr Wi lOOA yQUl WNO hQYrOpHYg NQHp
WNQW _hieMr_ QMhQcB gOW HYWi NOp OcOB—QYr BWHMM QB BNO MHBWOYOr, ip
BOOFOr Wi MHBWOY, WNO hNiMO AMQUO QpieYr NOp yOUQFO QMHLO hHWN WNO
BWpQYgO UpOQWepOB ix NOp MHWWMO BHBWOp’B rpOQF.

aNO MiYg gpQBB peBWMOr QW NOp xOOW QB WNO sNHWO VQyyHW NeppHOr yc—WNO
xpHgNWOYOr mieBO BAMQBNOr NHB hQc WNpiegN WNO YOHgNyiepHYg AiiM—BNO
UieMr NOQp WNO pQWWMO ix WNO WOQUeAB QB WNO mQpUN nQpO QYr NHB xpHOYrB
BNQpOr WNOHp YOLOp-OYrHYg FOQM, QYr WNO BNpHMM LiHUO ix WNO DeOOY
iprOpHYg ixx NOp eYxipWeYQWO geOBWB Wi OXOUeWHiY—iYUO FipO WNO AHg-yQyc
hQB BYOOEHYg iY WNO IeUNOBB’B lYOO, hNHMO AMQWOB QYr rHBNOB UpQBNOr
QpieYr HW—iYUO FipO WNO BNpHOl ix WNO qpcANiY, WNO BueOQlHYg ix WNO
RHEQpr’B BMQWO-AOYUHM, QYr WNO UNilHYg ix WNO BeAApOBBOr geHYOQ-AHgB,
xHMMOr WNO QHp, FHXOr eA hHWN WNO rHBWQYW BiyB ix WNO FHBOpQyMO miUl
aepWMO.

Si BNO BQW iY, hHWN UMiBOr OcOB, QYr NQMx yOMHOLOr NOpBOMx HY
siYrOpMQYr, WNiegN BNO lYOh BNO NQr yeW Wi iAOY WNOF QgQHY, QYr QMM
hieMr UNQYgO Wi reMM pOQMHWc—WNO gpQBB hieMr yO iYMc peBWMHYg HY WNO
hHYr, QYr WNO AiiM pHAAMHYg Wi WNO hQLHYg ix WNO pOOrB—WNO pQWWMHYg
WOQUeAB hieMr UNQYgO Wi WHYlMHYg BNOOA-yOMMB, QYr WNO DeOOY’B BNpHMM
UpHOB Wi WNO LiHUO ix WNO BNOANOpr yic—QYr WNO BYOOEO ix WNO yQyc, WNO
BNpHOl ix WNO qpcANiY, QYr QMM WNO iWNOp ueOOp YiHBOB, hieMr UNQYgO
(BNO lYOh) Wi WNO UiYxeBOr UMQFiep ix WNO yeBc xQpF-cQpr—hNHMO WNO
MihHYg ix WNO UQWWMO HY WNO rHBWQYUO hieMr WQlO WNO AMQUO ix WNO miUl
aepWMO’B NOQLc BiyB.

RQBWMc, BNO AHUWepOr Wi NOpBOMx Nih WNHB BQFO MHWWMO BHBWOp ix NOpB
hieMr, HY WNO QxWOp-WHFO, yO NOpBOMx Q gpihY hiFQY; QYr Nih BNO hieMr
lOOA, WNpiegN QMM NOp pHAOp cOQpB, WNO BHFAMO QYr MiLHYg NOQpW ix NOp
UNHMrNiir: QYr Nih BNO hieMr gQWNOp QyieW NOp iWNOp MHWWMO UNHMrpOY,
QYr FQlO _WNOHp_ OcOB ypHgNW QYr OQgOp hHWN FQYc Q BWpQYgO WQMO,

qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hiplB

1.z. Cc pOQrHYg ip eBHYg QYc AQpW ix WNHB fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF
OMOUWpiYHU hipl, cie HYrHUQWO WNQW cie NQLO pOQr, eYrOpBWQYr, QgpOO Wi
QYr QUUOAW QMM WNO WOpFB ix WNHB MHUOYBO QYr HYWOMMOUWeQM ApiAOpWc
(WpQrOFQpl/UiAcpHgNW) QgpOOFOYW. Zx cie ri YiW QgpOO Wi QyHrO yc QMM

rOBWpic QMM UiAHOB ix fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hiplB HY ciep
AiBBOBBHiY. Zx cie AQHr Q xOO xip iyWQHYHYg Q UiAc ix ip QUUOBB Wi Q
fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hipl QYr cie ri YiW QgpOO Wi yO yieYr

AOpBiY ip OYWHWc Wi hNiF cie AQHr WNO xOO QB BOW xipWN HY AQpQgpQAN
1.j.8.

1.C. "fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg" HB Q pOgHBWOpOr WpQrOFQpl. ZW FQc iYMc yO
eBOr iY ip QBBiUHQWOr HY QYc hQc hHWN QY OMOUWpiYHU hipl yc AOiAMO hNi

OLOY hHWNieW UiFAMcHYg hHWN WNO xeMM WOpFB ix WNHB QgpOOFOYW. SOO
AQpQgpQAN 1.w yOMih. aNOpO QpO Q MiW ix WNHYgB cie UQY ri hHWN fpikOUW
qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hiplB Hx cie xiMMih WNO WOpFB ix WNHB
QgpOOFOYW QYr NOMA ApOBOpLO xpOO xeWepO QUUOBB Wi fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF
OMOUWpiYHU hiplB. SOO AQpQgpQAN 1.j yOMih.

1.w. aNO fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg RHWOpQpc zpUNHLO PieYrQWHiY ("WNO
PieYrQWHiY" ip fqRzP), ihYB Q UiFAHMQWHiY UiAcpHgNW HY WNO UiMMOUWHiY
ix fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hiplB. GOQpMc QMM WNO HYrHLHreQM
hiplB HY WNO UiMMOUWHiY QpO HY WNO AeyMHU riFQHY HY WNO vYHWOr
SWQWOB. Zx QY HYrHLHreQM hipl HB eYApiWOUWOr yc UiAcpHgNW MQh HY WNO
vYHWOr SWQWOB QYr cie QpO MiUQWOr HY WNO vYHWOr SWQWOB, hO ri YiW
UMQHF Q pHgNW Wi ApOLOYW cie xpiF UiAcHYg, rHBWpHyeWHYg, AOpxipFHYg,
rHBAMQcHYg ip UpOQWHYg rOpHLQWHLO hiplB yQBOr iY WNO hipl QB MiYg QB
QMM pOxOpOYUOB Wi fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg QpO pOFiLOr. bx UiepBO, hO NiAO
WNQW cie hHMM BeAAipW WNO fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF FHBBHiY ix ApiFiWHYg
xpOO QUUOBB Wi OMOUWpiYHU hiplB yc xpOOMc BNQpHYg fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF

fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF YQFO QBBiUHQWOr hHWN WNO hipl. Tie UQY OQBHMc
UiFAMc hHWN WNO WOpFB ix WNHB QgpOOFOYW yc lOOAHYg WNHB hipl HY WNO
BQFO xipFQW hHWN HWB QWWQUNOr xeMM fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF RHUOYBO hNOY
cie BNQpO HW hHWNieW UNQpgO hHWN iWNOpB.

1.I. aNO UiAcpHgNW MQhB ix WNO AMQUO hNOpO cie QpO MiUQWOr QMBi giLOpY
hNQW cie UQY ri hHWN WNHB hipl. wiAcpHgNW MQhB HY FiBW UieYWpHOB QpO

QgpOOFOYW yOxipO rihYMiQrHYg, UiAcHYg, rHBAMQcHYg, AOpxipFHYg,
rHBWpHyeWHYg ip UpOQWHYg rOpHLQWHLO hiplB yQBOr iY WNHB hipl ip QYc
iWNOp fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF hipl. aNO PieYrQWHiY FQlOB Yi

1.j. vYMOBB cie NQLO pOFiLOr QMM pOxOpOYUOB Wi fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg:

1.j.1. aNO xiMMihHYg BOYWOYUO, hHWN QUWHLO MHYlB Wi, ip iWNOp
HFFOrHQWO QUUOBB Wi, WNO xeMM fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF RHUOYBO FeBW QAAOQp
ApiFHYOYWMc hNOYOLOp QYc UiAc ix Q fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF hipl (QYc hipl

AOpxipFOr, LHOhOr, UiAHOr ip rHBWpHyeWOr:

  aNHB OCiil HB xip WNO eBO ix QYciYO QYchNOpO HY WNO vYHWOr SWQWOB QYr
  FiBW iWNOp AQpWB ix WNO hipMr QW Yi UiBW QYr hHWN QMFiBW Yi
  pOBWpHUWHiYB hNQWBiOLOp. Tie FQc UiAc HW, gHLO HW QhQc ip pO-eBO HW

1.j.2. Zx QY HYrHLHreQM fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF OMOUWpiYHU hipl HB
rOpHLOr xpiF WOXWB YiW ApiWOUWOr yc v.S. UiAcpHgNW MQh (riOB YiW

WNO vYHWOr SWQWOB hHWNieW AQcHYg QYc xOOB ip UNQpgOB. Zx cie QpO

UiFApOBBOr, FQplOr eA, YiYApiApHOWQpc ip ApiApHOWQpc xipF, HYUMerHYg

  WNO eBO ix fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg-WF hiplB UQMUeMQWOr eBHYg WNO FOWNir

  SOUWHiY 4, "ZYxipFQWHiY QyieW riYQWHiYB Wi WNO fpikOUW qeWOYyOpg
  RHWOpQpc zpUNHLO PieYrQWHiY."

* Tie ApiLHrO Q xeMM pOxeYr ix QYc FiYOc AQHr yc Q eBOp hNi YiWHxHOB
  cie HY hpHWHYg (ip yc O-FQHM) hHWNHY 30 rQcB ix pOUOHAW WNQW B/NO

1.j.9. Zx cie hHBN Wi UNQpgO Q xOO ip rHBWpHyeWO Q fpikOUW
